David was then sent in to treat areas that were affected by termites. The customer service with CPC is out of this world. They know their stuff! <Review>I have to admit, I always thought I was one who couldn't handle spice...even the chili dust from eating popcorn chicken would set my mouth ablaze. With that being said, I never really enjoyed hot chicken sandwiches to it's full potential; I always opted for 'non-spicy'. My life changed 180 when I decided to give Chicken as Cluck's Nashville hot chicken sandwich a try...with ACTUAL spice! Oh My Goodness, the sandwich was sooo good! Although it was mild-medium spicy, it was a just the right amount spice that just meets my threshold. The chicken meat was very moist and the brioche bun was the perfect carrier. I gobbled it up and enjoyed every bite. To accompany the sandwich, I ordered sweet potato fries, which have a panko batter coating. This is great as the fries are extra crispy. Who doesn't love a good crunch?!

I'm glad that Chicken as Cluck was my gateway sandwich to the Nashville hot chicken sandwich world.</Review>< pics>

<review>Nice little Asian fusion spot in Coronado. I came in towards the end of the evening and got a table by the window so I could people watch. My waiter, Jack, was fantastic and very attentive without being intrusive. I ordered the Mongolian beef and a side of garlic noodles. Jack suggested having the kitchen put them together instead of served separately, which was a good idea (since I was going to do that anyway). I also got a side of dumplings and a cocktail. My main course was excellent and the cocktail was made with a generous amount of booze ;) the dumplings were OK, but I've had better. Other than the dumplings it was a great meal. Although were I'm from this place would be considered a bit pricey, but for this area I would say the prices are reasonable. Definitely recommend this place!<//review><pics>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPDM7YGf69_gI4ZmVgSlLm2RDP55_7KJgquugFO=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipPSPRFmE-OzQ7_p0SZtcY_M759kGwYoiRp-njJN=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOEcgcU1rp5CfBdBzuZbcWVuV6KA5yAcskfI8PT=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]<//pics><user>104477197896483046104< /user><gmap_id>0x80deaccc1a2f2ccb:0x3838db7647b13c23<//gmap_id><Name>Bill Chenoweth< /Name><Date>1536778587943<//Date>< response>

<review>We were walking along Coronado and wanted to check out a place for dinner. The menu looked good, so we just walked in. Waited about 5 mins before we got a table. I have to mention, as a side note, that our server, a pleasant older American gentleman, was extremely sweet!
I chose the warm sake. I've had better elsewhere, but I liked it. For food, we chose the Coronado Sushi and the pan fried rice noodles. The sushi was DELICIOUS. I'm not much of a sushi person unless they are spicy and do not have seaweed. This one hit all the right flavours! The wasabi was good. The crab in the sushi was very moist.  The pan fried noodles were pretty great too. Came with a bunch of veggies and beef. And although they were fried, they were soft and didn't make you feel bloated later. Amongst the two of us, we got these 2 plates and couldn't finish the noodles fully. The ambience is nice. If you love flavours and smell of spices, see if you can get a seat at the sushi counter or close to it. Good spot. Will be back.</review>< date>

We shared the chicken chow me in, which came with rice and a salad and we added a cup of egg drop soup and tropical iced tea to drink. The tea was the best part of the meal.
